1. A 6-year-old boy with congenital heart disease (pulmonary artery stenosis) presents with suppurative periostitis of the maxilla. The child needs surgical treatment. What unit should he be referred to?
*a. The pediatric maxillofacial unit
b. The out-patient unit after preliminary cardiological treatment
c. The out-patient or in-patient unit at the discretion of the child's parents
d. The cardiology unit
e. The out-patient unit, no precautions are necessary

2. An implant-supported removable denture is planned to be made for a 70-year-old patient to replace a complete defect in the lower dentition. Objectively, the alveolar processes of both jaws are significantly atrophied, the edentulous jaws are positioned in an orthognathic bite. What minimum number of implants is required for fixation of the denture in this case?
*a. 2
b. 8
c. 4
d. 6
e. 1

3. A 62-year-old man came to a dentist to have his tooth 44 extracted. During examination he suddenly fell unconscious. His breathing and pulse are slow, his head is bowed, his arms are flexed in the elbows and wrists, his legs are stretched out, and his jaws are clenched tight. The patient developed clonic convulsion and started foaming at the mouth. His pupils are dilated and unresponsive to light. 1.5 minutes later, the patient's muscles relaxed. The patient is mentally confused. What is the most likely diagnosis in this case?
*a. Epileptic seizure
b. Paroxysmal tachycardia attack
c. Syncope
d. Acute cerebrovascular accident
e. Hypertensive crisis

4. During examination the child presents with retracted mucosa on the soft palate and uvula. The child was diagnosed with congenital submucous cleft soft palate. What surgical operation is necessary in this case?
a. Uranoplasty
*b. Veloplasty
c. Rhinocheiloplasty
d. Uranostaphyloplasty
e. Cheiloplasty

5. A 15-year-old boy fell from a bicycle and hit his face. He came to a doctor for medical aid. After examination, the doctor established that the patient had a closed mechanical injury of the soft tissues without any visible violation of their anatomical integrity. Make the diagnosis.
a. Abrasion
*b. Contusion
c. Wound
d. Bruise
e. Hematoma

6. What period of bite formation in a child can be normally characterized by physiological tremata and diastemata?

b. Formation of milk occlusion (6 months - 3 years)
c. It is always a sign of pathology
d. Changing occlusion
e. Permanent occlusion

8. A 15-year-old patient complains of bleeding gums and pain during eating. These signs have been observed for the last year. Objectively the interdental papillae in the area of teeth 31, 32, 33, 41, 42, and 43 are enlarged and cover the tooth crowns by 1/2 of their height. The gums present with bright-red granulations and are painful on palpation. Mineralized dental plaque is observed on the teeth. X-ray shows no changes of the alveolar process. What is the most likely diagnosis?
*a. Hypertrophic gingivitis
b. Generalized periodontitis
c. Ulcerative gingivitis
d. Catarrhal gingivitis
e. Localized periodontitis

9. The mother of a 3-year-old boy complains of an increase in his body temperature to 39^oC, sharply painful small wounds in his mouth, and excessive salivation. Objectively, the gums are hyperemic, edematous, and bleeding. On the hard palate and mucosa of the cheeks and lips, there are numerous small oval erosions up to 2 mm in diameter with whitish coating. *d. Acute herpetic stomatitis

Objectively, on the vestibular surface of teeth 11, 12, 13, 21, 22, 23, 31, 32, 33, 41, 42, and 43 there are defects of hard tissues, with softened dark pigmented dentin. b. Cuneiform defect
c. Acute median caries
d. Systemic enamel hypoplasia
e. Erosion of hard dental tissues

b. Pterygomaxillary space abscess

*d. Pericoronitis of tooth 38
e. Acute odontogenic periostitis

858. A 21-year-old man came to the dentist complaining of general weakness, muscle pain, body temperature up to 38.3^oC, indigestion, excessive salivation, and rashes in the oral and nasal cavities, urethra, on the wings of the nose, and in the interdigital folds.
